# Repos Create-for-Authenticated-User

Creates a new repository for the authenticated user.

**OAuth scope requirements**

When using [OAuth](https://docs.github.com/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/), authorizations must include:

* `public_repo` scope or `repo` scope to create a public repository. Note: For GitHub AE, use `repo` scope to create an internal repository.
* `repo` scope to create a private repository.

API method documentation: [https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/repos#create-a-repository-for-the-authenticated-user](https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/repos#create-a-repository-for-the-authenticated-user)

```java
CompletableFuture<UserReposResponse> reposCreateForAuthenticatedUserAsync(
    final UserReposRequest body)
```

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `body` | [`UserReposRequest`](../../doc/models/user-repos-request.md) | Body, Required | - |

## Response Type

[`UserReposResponse`](../../doc/models/user-repos-response.md)

## Example Usage

```java
UserReposRequest body = new UserReposRequest();
body.setName("Hello-World");
body.setDescription("This is your first repo!");
body.setHomepage("https://github.com");
body.setPrivate(false);
body.setIsTemplate(true);

reposController.reposCreateForAuthenticatedUserAsync(body).thenAccept(result -> {
    // TODO success callback handler
}).exceptionally(exception -> {
    // TODO failure callback handler
    return null;
});
```

| 403 | Forbidden | [`UserRepos403ErrorException`](../../doc/models/user-repos-403-error-exception.md) |
| 404 | Resource not found | [`UserRepos404ErrorException`](../../doc/models/user-repos-404-error-exception.md) |
| 422 | Validation failed, or the endpoint has been spammed. | [`UserRepos422ErrorException`](../../doc/models/user-repos-422-error-exception.md) |


# Repos List-Invitations-for-Authenticated-User

When authenticating as a user, this endpoint will list all currently open repository invitations for that user.

API method documentation: [https://docs.github.com/rest/collaborators/invitations#list-repository-invitations-for-the-authenticated-user](https://docs.github.com/rest/collaborators/invitations#list-repository-invitations-for-the-authenticated-user)

```java
CompletableFuture<List<RepositoryInvitation>> reposListInvitationsForAuthenticatedUserAsync(
    final Integer perPage,
    final Integer page)
```

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `perPage` | `Integer` | Query, Optional | The number of results per page (max 100).<br>**Default**: `30` |
| `page` | `Integer` | Query, Optional | Page number of the results to fetch.<br>**Default**: `1` |

## Response Type

[`List<RepositoryInvitation>`](../../doc/models/repository-invitation.md)

## Example Usage

```java
Integer perPage = 30;
Integer page = 1;

reposController.reposListInvitationsForAuthenticatedUserAsync(perPage, page).thenAccept(result -> {
    // TODO success callback handler
}).exceptionally(exception -> {
    // TODO failure callback handler
    return null;
});
```

# Repos List-for-User

Lists public repositories for the specified user. Note: For GitHub AE, this endpoint will list internal repositories for the specified user.

API method documentation: [https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/repos#list-repositories-for-a-user](https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/repos#list-repositories-for-a-user)

```java
CompletableFuture<List<MinimalRepository>> reposListForUserAsync(
    final String username,
    final Type6161Enum type,
    final Sort61Enum sort,
    final Direction21Enum direction,
    final Integer perPage,
    final Integer page)
```

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `username` | `String` | Template, Required | The handle for the GitHub user account. |
| `type` | [`Type6161Enum`](../../doc/models/type-6161-enum.md) | Query, Optional | Limit results to repositories of the specified type. |
| `sort` | [`Sort61Enum`](../../doc/models/sort-61-enum.md) | Query, Optional | The property to sort the results by. |
| `direction` | [`Direction21Enum`](../../doc/models/direction-21-enum.md) | Query, Optional | The order to sort by. Default: `asc` when using `full_name`, otherwise `desc`. |
| `perPage` | `Integer` | Query, Optional | The number of results per page (max 100).<br>**Default**: `30` |
| `page` | `Integer` | Query, Optional | Page number of the results to fetch.<br>**Default**: `1` |

## Response Type

[`List<MinimalRepository>`](../../doc/models/minimal-repository.md)

## Example Usage

```java
String username = "username0";
Integer perPage = 30;
Integer page = 1;

reposController.reposListForUserAsync(username, null, null, null, perPage, page).thenAccept(result -> {
    // TODO success callback handler
}).exceptionally(exception -> {
    // TODO failure callback handler
    return null;
});
```
